# ВЕТКА ТУРКА
###########################

add_namespace = NWturkey
add_namespace = NW_new_turkey

#Претензии на Хатай // FRA
country_event = {
	id = NWturkey.1
	title = NWturkey.1.t
	desc = NWturkey.1.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_tur_ataturk_writing_desk
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NWturkey.1" }
	
	#Оставить Хатай частью Сирии 
	option = {
		name = NWturkey.1.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
		}
		add_named_threat = { threat = 3 name = TUR_claims_hatay_threat1_tt }
		add_opinion_modifier = { target = FROM modifier = diplomatic_affront }
		FROM = { add_opinion_modifier = { target = ROOT modifier = diplomatic_affront } }
	}
	#Предоставить автономию Хатаю
	option = {
		name = NWturkey.1.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				has_war = yes
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				945 = {
					controller = {
						has_full_control_of_state = PREV
						OR = {
							tag = event_target:NW_france_scope
							is_subject_of = event_target:NW_france_scope
						}
					}
				}
			}
			HAT = {
				add_state_core = 945
				transfer_state = 945
				event_target:NW_france_scope = {
					puppet = HAT
					set_autonomy = { target = HAT autonomy_state = autonomy_integrated_puppet }
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					add_ideas = HAT_near_autonomy_status
					set_cosmetic_tag = HAT_SANDJAK
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				SYR = {
					has_full_control_of_state = 945
					NOT = { is_subject_of = event_target:NW_france_scope }
				}
			}
			HAT = {
				add_state_core = 945
				transfer_state = 945
				SYR = {
					puppet = HAT
					set_autonomy = { target = HAT autonomy_state = autonomy_integrated_puppet }
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					add_ideas = HAT_near_autonomy_status
					set_cosmetic_tag = HAT_SANDJAK
				}
			}
		}
		add_named_threat = { threat = -3 name = TUR_claims_hatay_threat2_tt }
		FROM = {
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = democratic
				popularity = 0.02
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { SYR = { exists = yes } }
			SYR = { country_event = { id = NWturkey.73 } }
		}
	}
}


#Монтрё. Приглашение
country_event = {
	id = NWturkey.2
	title = NWturkey.2.t
	desc = NWturkey.2.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_tur_the_montreux_convention
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NWturkey.2" }
	
	#Согласиться на переговоры
	option = {
		name = NWturkey.2.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 90
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				tag = ITA
				has_government = fascism
				has_global_flag = NW_TUR_OLD_FOCUS_TREE
			}
		}
		country_event = { id = NWturkey.3 days = 1 }
		set_country_flag = montreux_member_flag
	}
	#Отказаться 
	option = {
		name = NWturkey.2.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				tag = ITA
				has_government = fascism
				FROM = { has_idea = TUR_fascist_grand_council }
			}
		}
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = FROM
			modifier = TUR_the_montreux_convention_cancel
		}
		FROM = {
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = ROOT
				modifier = TUR_the_montreux_convention_cancel
			}
		}
	}
}

#Монтрё. Голосование
country_event = {
	id = NWturkey.3
	title = NWturkey.3.t
	desc = NWturkey.3.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_tur_the_montreux_convention
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NWturkey.3" }
	
	#Оставить зону демилитаризированной 
	option = {
		name = NWturkey.3.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				tag = ITA
				TUR = { has_idea = TUR_fascist_grand_council }
			}
		}
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = TUR
			modifier = TUR_the_montreux_convention_abort_demilitariz
		}
		TUR = {
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = ROOT
				modifier = TUR_the_montreux_convention_abort_demilitariz
			}
		}
	}
	#Ремилитаризация зоны 
	option = {
		name = NWturkey.3.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 75
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				NOT = { tag = ITA }
				TUR = { has_idea = TUR_fascist_grand_council }
			}
		}
		TUR = { add_to_variable = { montreux_score = 1 } }
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = TUR
			modifier = TUR_the_montreux_convention_accept_demilitariz
		}
		TUR = {
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = ROOT
				modifier = TUR_the_montreux_convention_accept_demilitariz
			}
		}
	}
}

#Монтрё. Итог у турка
country_event = {
	id = NWturkey.4
	title = NWturkey.4.t
	desc = NWturkey.4.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_tur_the_montreux_convention
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NWturkey.4" }
	
	#Таки ремилитаризация
	option = {
		name = NWturkey.4.a
		trigger = {
			TUR = { check_variable = { var = montreux_score value = 5 compare = greater_than_or_equals } }
		}
		341 = { set_demilitarized_zone = no }
		964 = { set_demilitarized_zone = no }
	}
	#Таки слив
	option = {
		name = NWturkey.4.b
		trigger = {
			TUR = { check_variable = { montreux_score < 5 } }
		}
		set_country_flag = dem_montreux_denied
	}
}

#Аннексия Хатая
country_event = {
	id = NWturkey.5
	title = NWturkey.5.t
	desc = NWturkey.5.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_tur_ataturk_writing_desk
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NWturkey.5" }
	
	option = {
		name = NWturkey.5.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 90
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				has_war = yes
			}
		}
		TUR = { transfer_state = 945 }
	}
	option = {
		name = NWturkey.5.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 90
			modifier = {
				AND = {
					event_target:NW_france_scope = { has_government = democratic }
					GER = { has_government = fascism }
					threat > 0.39
				}
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				AND = {
					event_target:NW_france_scope = { has_government = democratic }
					GER = { has_government = fascism }
					event_target:NW_france_scope = { has_war_with = GER }
				}
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				TUR = { is_in_faction_with = event_target:NW_france_scope }
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				event_target:NW_france_scope = { is_in_faction_with = ENG }
				ENG = { has_guaranteed = TUR }
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				FROM = { has_government = ROOT }
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		TUR = { transfer_state = 945 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				TUR = { is_in_faction_with = ENG }
				event_target:NW_france_scope = { 
					is_in_faction_with = ENG
					is_faction_leader = no
				}
			}
			event_target:NW_france_scope = { leave_faction = yes }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { owns_state = 945 } }
			945 = {
				owner = {
					TUR = {
						declare_war_on = {
							type = take_state_focus
							target = PREV
							generator = { 945 }
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { TUR = { NOT = { has_country_flag = tur_hatay_peace_flag } } }
				TUR = { country_event = { id = NWturkey.74 months = 1 } }
			}
		}
	}
}

	id = NWturkey.6
	title = NWturkey.6.t
	desc = NWturkey.6.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_tur_ataturk_inonu_parliament
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = NWturkey.6.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				tag = GER
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
				has_global_flag = NW_TUR_OLD_FOCUS_TREE
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1000
				tag = ENG
				OR = {
					GER = {
						exists = yes
						OR = {
							has_government = monarchy
							has_government = fascism
						}
					}
					SOV = {
						exists = yes
						has_government = communism
					}
				}
				has_global_flag = NW_TUR_OLD_FOCUS_TREE
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				tag = ENG
				FROM = { has_government = fascism }
				has_global_flag = NW_TUR_OLD_FOCUS_TREE
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1000
				tag = GER
				OR = {
					ENG = {
						exists = yes
						has_government = democratic
					}
					SOV = {
						exists = yes

					}
				}

		}

		FROM = { country_event = { id = NWturkey.8 days = 1 } }
	}
}

	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NWturkey.9" }

	option = {
		name = NWturkey.9.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = var:current_party_ideology_group
			popularity = -0.1
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = democratic
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = fascism
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = communism
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		add_manpower = -5000
		add_stability = 0.05
	}
	
	option = {
		name = NWturkey.9.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = var:current_party_ideology_group
			popularity = -0.05
		}
		
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = democratic
			popularity = 0.03
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = fascism
			popularity = 0.03
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = communism
			popularity = 0.03
		}
	}
}

#Смерть Ататюрка пульсар // 10 ноября 1938 года
country_event = {
	id = NWturkey.1000
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hidden = yes
	
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NWturkey.1000" }
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_global_flag = ataturk_dead }
			}
			country_event = { id = NWturkey.10 }
		}
	}
}

# Смерть Ататюрка // 10 ноября 1938 года
country_event = {
	id = NWturkey.10
	title = NWturkey.10.t
	desc = NWturkey.10.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_tur_ataturk_death
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NWturkey.10" }
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_global_flag = ataturk_dead
			if = {
				limit = { neutrality > 0.2 }
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = neutrality
					popularity = -0.1
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_ai = yes
					NOT = {
						has_completed_focus = TUR_president_ismet_inenu
						has_completed_focus = TUR_dictatorship_cakmak
						has_completed_focus = TUR_power_of_special_services
						has_completed_focus = TUR_recep_peker
						has_completed_focus = TUR_organize_fair_elections
						has_completed_focus = TUR_etchem_circassian_coup
						has_completed_focus = TUR_commust_revolt
						has_completed_focus = TUR_force_of_order
					}
					OR = {
						has_country_flag = NW_TUR_AI_NEUTRAL
						has_country_flag = NW_TUR_AI_NEUTRAL_ALTERNATE
						is_historical_focus_on = yes
					}
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = neutrality
					popularity = 0.42
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_ai = yes
					NOT = {
						has_completed_focus = TUR_president_ismet_inenu
						has_completed_focus = TUR_dictatorship_cakmak
						has_completed_focus = TUR_power_of_special_services
						has_completed_focus = TUR_recep_peker
						has_completed_focus = TUR_organize_fair_elections
						has_completed_focus = TUR_etchem_circassian_coup
						has_completed_focus = TUR_commust_revolt
						has_completed_focus = TUR_force_of_order
					}
					OR = {
						has_country_flag = NW_TUR_AI_DEMOCRATIC
						has_country_flag = NW_TUR_AI_FASCIST
						has_country_flag = NW_TUR_AI_TROZKIST
						has_country_flag = NW_TUR_AI_COMMUNIST
						has_country_flag = NW_TUR_AI_COMMUNIST_ALTERNATE
						has_country_flag = NW_TUR_AI_DEMOCRATIC_ALTERNATE
						has_country_flag = NW_TUR_AI_MONARCHY
					}
					is_historical_focus_on = no
					neutrality > 0.399
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = neutrality
					popularity = -1
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = neutrality
					popularity = 0.15
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = NWturkey.10.a
		capital_scope = { add_manpower = -1 }
		if = {
			limit = { neutrality > 0.2 }
			effect_tooltip = {
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = neutrality
					popularity = -0.1
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_leader = {
					character = TUR_mustafa_kemal_ataturk
					ruling_only = yes 
				} 
			}
			kill_country_leader = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_unit_leader = 59 }
			remove_unit_leader = 59
		}
		create_country_leader = {
			name = "Mustafa Abdülhalik Renda"
			desc = "POLITICS_MUSTAFA_ABDÜLHALIK_RENDA_DESC"
			picture = "Portrait_Baskani_Abdulhalik_Renda.dds"
			expire = "1965.1.1"
			ideology = kemalism
			traits = {
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_subject = no
				NOT = {
					has_completed_focus = TUR_president_ismet_inenu
					has_completed_focus = TUR_dictatorship_cakmak
					has_completed_focus = TUR_power_of_special_services
					has_completed_focus = TUR_recep_peker
					has_completed_focus = TUR_organize_fair_elections
					has_completed_focus = TUR_etchem_circassian_coup
					has_completed_focus = TUR_commust_revolt
					has_completed_focus = TUR_force_of_order
				}
				NOT = {
					has_global_flag = WORLD_OF_SPLIT_FLAG
					has_global_flag = THE_MOTHER_OF_ORDER_FLAG
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = TUR_president_ismet_inenu_flag
				}
				country_event = { id = NWturkey.30 days = 2 }
			
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						has_country_flag = TUR_dictatorship_cakmak_flag
					}
					country_event = { id = NWturkey.81 days = 2 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						has_country_flag = TUR_policy_liberalization_flag
					}
					country_event = { id = NWturkey.82 days = 2 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						has_country_flag = TUR_power_of_special_services_flag
					}
					country_event = { id = NWturkey.83 days = 2 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						has_country_flag = TUR_recep_peker_flag
					}
					country_event = { id = NWturkey.84 days = 2 }
				}
			}
			
			if = {
				limit = { neutrality < 0.4 }
				country_event = { id = NWturkey.29 days = 3 }
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = { news_event = { id = trworldnews.55 hours = 6 } }
	}
}


#Пантюркизм
country_event = {
	id = NWturkey.11
	title = NWturkey.11.t
	desc = NWturkey.11.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_tur_kurds_traditionalists_thwarted
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NWturkey.11" }

	option = {
		name = NWturkey.11.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 75
		}
		diplomatic_relation = {
			country = FROM
			relation = guarantee
			active = no
		}
		FROM = {
			diplomatic_relation = {
				country = ROOT
				relation = guarantee
				active = no
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction_with = FROM
				FROM = { is_faction_leader = yes }
			}
			leave_faction = yes
		}
		add_threat = 1
	}
	
	option = {
		name = NWturkey.11.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
		}
	}
}

#Месть Турана // PER
country_event = {
	id = NWturkey.12
	title = NWturkey.12.t
	desc = NWturkey.12.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_rally_3
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NWturkey.12" }

	option = {
		name = NWturkey.12.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
		}
		419 = { add_core_of = FROM }
		963 = { add_core_of = FROM }
		FROM = {
			transfer_state = 419
			transfer_state = 963
		}
		diplomatic_relation = {
			country = FROM
			relation = military_access
			active = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { is_subject_of = ROOT } }
			FROM = {
				add_autonomy_score = {
					value = -250
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = NWturkey.12.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}
		FROM = { country_event = { id = NWturkey.13 days = 1 } }
		custom_effect_tooltip = NWturkey_12_b_tt
	}
	
	option = {
		name = NWturkey.12.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 75
		}
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { NOT = { is_subject_of = ROOT } } }
			419 = { add_claim_by = FROM }
			963 = { add_claim_by = FROM }
			if = {
				limit = { has_guaranteed = FROM }
				diplomatic_relation = {
					country = FROM
					relation = guarantee
					active = no
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { is_guaranteed_by = FROM }
				FROM = {
					diplomatic_relation = {
						country = ROOT
						relation = guarantee
						active = no
					}
				}
			}
			FROM = {
				create_wargoal = {
					type = take_state_focus
					target = ROOT
					generator = { 419 963 }
				}
				add_ai_strategy = {
					type = conquer
					id = ROOT
					value = 200
				}
				add_ai_strategy = {
					type = antagonize
					id = ROOT
					value = 200
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_in_faction_with = FROM
					FROM = { is_faction_leader = yes }
				}
				leave_faction = yes
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { is_subject_of = ROOT } }
			FROM = {
				add_autonomy_score = {
					value = 250
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = NWturkey.16
	title = NWturkey.16.t
	desc = NWturkey.16.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_rally_3
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NWturkey.16" }

	option = {
		name = NWturkey.16.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 100
				ENG = { has_war = yes }
				ENG = {
					OR = {
						surrender_progress > 0.65
						has_capitulated = yes
					}
				}
				GRE = { is_in_faction_with = ENG }
			}
		}
		release_puppet = CYP
	}
	option = {
		name = NWturkey.16.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 100
				ENG = { has_war = no }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 100
				ENG = { surrender_progress < 0.01 }
			}
		}
		add_stability = -0.03
		release = NCP
		NCP = {
			declare_war_on = {
				target = ENG
				type = annex_everything
			}
		}
		TUR = { country_event = { id = NWturkey.17 days = 1 } }
	}
	option = {
		name = NWturkey.16.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 100
				ENG = { has_war = yes }
				ENG = {
					OR = {
						surrender_progress > 0.65
						has_capitulated = yes
					}
				}
				GRE = { NOT = { is_in_faction_with = ENG } }
			}
		}
		GRE = { country_event = { id = NWturkey.19 days = 1 } }
		183 = { add_core_of = GRE }
		772 = { add_core_of = GRE }
		1153 = { add_core_of = GRE }
		GRE = {
			transfer_state = 183
			transfer_state = 772
			transfer_state = 1153
		}
	}
}

	}

		custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_civwar_tt
		hidden_effect = {

							843 = { controller = { OR = { original_tag = ROOT is_subject_of = ROOT } } }
							964 = { controller = { OR = { original_tag = ROOT is_subject_of = ROOT } } }
						}
						OR = {
							state = 341
							state = 843
							state = 964
						}
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							342 = { controller = { OR = { original_tag = ROOT is_subject_of = ROOT } } }
							1167 = { controller = { OR = { original_tag = ROOT is_subject_of = ROOT } } }
							343 = { controller = { OR = { original_tag = ROOT is_subject_of = ROOT } } }
							339 = { controller = { OR = { original_tag = ROOT is_subject_of = ROOT } } }
							340 = { controller = { OR = { original_tag = ROOT is_subject_of = ROOT } } }
						}
						OR = {
							state = 342
							state = 1167
							state = 343
							state = 339
						}
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							OR = {
								341 = { controller = { OR = { original_tag = ROOT is_subject_of = ROOT } } }
								843 = { controller = { OR = { original_tag = ROOT is_subject_of = ROOT } } }
								964 = { controller = { OR = { original_tag = ROOT is_subject_of = ROOT } } }

								343 = { controller = { OR = { original_tag = ROOT is_subject_of = ROOT } } }
								339 = { controller = { OR = { original_tag = ROOT is_subject_of = ROOT } } }
							}

							state = 341
							state = 843
							state = 964
							state = 342
							state = 1167
							state = 343
							state = 339
						}
					}
				}
			}

					has_government = fascism
				}
				#add_ideas = TUR_civil_war

				set_country_flag = same_ideology_civil_war_flag

					neutrality = 95
					fascism = 5
				}

					ruling_party = neutrality
					elections_allowed = no
				}

country_event = {
	id = NWturkey.33
	title = NWturkey.33.t
	desc = NWturkey.33.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_rally_3
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NWturkey.33" }

	option = {
		name = NWturkey.33.a
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_government = fascism }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				is_historical_focus_on = no
				OR = {
					any_country_with_original_tag = {
						original_tag_to_check = AUS
						has_country_flag = hbbrg_flag
						has_government = democratic
					}
					any_country_with_original_tag = {
						original_tag_to_check = HUN
						has_country_flag = hbbrg_flag
						has_government = democratic
					}
					any_country_with_original_tag = {
						original_tag_to_check = CZE
						has_country_flag = hbbrg_flag
						has_government = democratic
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_country_flag = NW_TUR_AI_FASCIST
			}
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = democratic
			popularity = 0.25
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = democratic
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
		hidden_effect = { news_event = { id = trworldnews.58 hours = 6 } }
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_faction_leader = yes
				has_completed_focus = TUR_create_the_sadabat_pact
				any_allied_country = {
					OR = {
						has_government = democratic
						has_government = neutrality
					}
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					is_in_faction_with = ROOT
					NOT = {
						has_government = democratic
						has_government = neutrality
					}
				}
				leave_faction = yes
				hidden_effect = {
					add_ai_strategy = {
						type = befriend
						id = ROOT
						value = -100
					}
					add_ai_strategy = {
						type = alliance
						id = ROOT
						value = -200
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							PER = {
								has_completed_focus = PER_cut_ties_with_europe
								is_faction_leader = yes
							}
						}
						add_ai_strategy = {
							type = befriend
							id = "PER"		
							value = 100
						}
						add_ai_strategy = {
							type = alliance
							id = "PER"
							value = 200
						}
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = TUR_dem_sadabad_flag } }
				set_country_flag = TUR_dem_sadabad_flag
				set_faction_name = TUR_dem_sadabad
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				is_faction_leader = yes
				any_allied_country = {
					NOT = {
						has_government = democratic
						has_government = neutrality
					}
				}
			}
			dismantle_faction = yes
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = NWturkey.33.b
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_government = democratic }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				is_historical_focus_on = no
				GER = { has_government = fascism }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				is_historical_focus_on = no
				OR = {
					any_country_with_original_tag = {
						original_tag_to_check = AUS
						has_country_flag = hbbrg_flag
						has_government = fascism
					}
					any_country_with_original_tag = {
						original_tag_to_check = HUN
						has_country_flag = hbbrg_flag
						has_government = fascism
					}
					any_country_with_original_tag = {
						original_tag_to_check = CZE
						has_country_flag = hbbrg_flag
						has_government = fascism
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_country_flag = NW_TUR_AI_DEMOCRATIC
			}
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = fascism
			popularity = 0.25
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = fascism
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
		hidden_effect = { news_event = { id = trworldnews.59 hours = 6 } }
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_faction_leader = yes
				has_completed_focus = TUR_create_the_sadabat_pact
				any_allied_country = {
					OR = {
						has_government = fascism
						has_government = monarchy
					}
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					is_in_faction_with = ROOT
					NOT = {
						has_government = fascism
						has_government = monarchy
					}
				}
				leave_faction = yes
				hidden_effect = {
					add_ai_strategy = {
						type = befriend
						id = ROOT
						value = -100
					}
					add_ai_strategy = {
						type = alliance
						id = ROOT
						value = -200
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							PER = {
								has_completed_focus = PER_cut_ties_with_europe
								is_faction_leader = yes
							}
						}
						add_ai_strategy = {
							type = befriend
							id = "PER"		
							value = 100
						}
						add_ai_strategy = {
							type = alliance
							id = "PER"
							value = 200
						}
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = TUR_dem_sadabad_flag } }
				set_faction_name = TUR_fas_sadabad
			}
			else = { set_faction_name = TUR_fas_sadabad_2 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				is_faction_leader = yes
				any_allied_country = {
					NOT = {
						has_government = fascism
						has_government = monarchy
					}
				}
			}
			dismantle_faction = yes
		}
	}
}

				has_country_flag = NW_TUR_AI_TROZKIST

							}

								OR = {
									341 = { controller = { OR = { original_tag = ROOT is_subject_of = ROOT } } }
									843 = { controller = { OR = { original_tag = ROOT is_subject_of = ROOT } } }
									964 = { controller = { OR = { original_tag = ROOT is_subject_of = ROOT } } }
									340 = { controller = { OR = { original_tag = ROOT is_subject_of = ROOT } } }
									342 = { controller = { OR = { original_tag = ROOT is_subject_of = ROOT } } }
									1167 = { controller = { OR = { original_tag = ROOT is_subject_of = ROOT } } }
									343 = { controller = { OR = { original_tag = ROOT is_subject_of = ROOT } } }
									339 = { controller = { OR = { original_tag = ROOT is_subject_of = ROOT } } }

country_event = {
	id = NWturkey.40
	title = NWturkey.40.t
	desc = NWturkey.40.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_tur_sultan_in_istanbul
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NWturkey.40" }

	option = {
		name = NWturkey.40.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				is_in_faction_with = ENG
				factor = 0.7
			}
			modifier = {
				GER = {
					OR = {
						has_government = democratic
						has_government = monarchy
					}
				}
				factor = 2
			}
			modifier = {
				OR = {
					any_country_with_original_tag = {
						original_tag_to_check = AUS
						has_country_flag = hbbrg_flag
					}
					any_country_with_original_tag = {
						original_tag_to_check = HUN
						has_country_flag = hbbrg_flag
					}
					any_country_with_original_tag = {
						original_tag_to_check = CZE
						has_country_flag = hbbrg_flag
					}
				}
				factor = 2
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = monarch_focus_block_flag
		add_stability = 0.05
		add_political_power = 100
		set_party_name = { ideology = democratic name = TUR_democratic_progressive_party long_name = TUR_democratic_progressive_party_long }
		set_party_name = { ideology = monarchy name = TUR_monarchy_force_of_order_party long_name = TUR_monarchy_force_of_order_party }
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = monarchy
			popularity = 0.2

#Смерть Абдул-Меджида II
country_event = {
	id = NWturkey.42
	title = NWturkey.42.t
	desc = NWturkey.42.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_tur_sultan_and_pashas
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NWturkey.42" }
	
	trigger = {
		original_tag = TUR
		date > 1944.01.01
	}

	option = {
		capital_scope = { add_manpower = -1 }
		name = NWturkey.42.a
		random_unit_leader = {
			limit = { has_id = 1801 }
			retire = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_government = monarchy }
			if = {
				limit = { has_idea = TUR_Abdulmejid_II }
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = TUR_Abdulmejid_II
					add_idea = TUR_Omer_Faruk_Osmanoglu
				}
			}
			add_stability = -0.05
		}
		else = {
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Omer Faruk Osmanoglu"
				desc = "POLITICS_OMER_FARUK_OSMANOGLU_DESC"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/TUR/Portrait_Omer_Faruk_Osmanoglu.dds"
				expire = "1965.1.1"
				ideology = absolute_monarchy
				traits = {
					keep_of_order
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

#Саадабад. ПОН
country_event = {
	id = NWturkey.43
	title = NWturkey.43.t
	desc = NWturkey.43.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_tur_the_saadabad_pact
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NWturkey.43" }
	
	option = {
		name = NWturkey.43.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { tag = TUR }
				TUR = { has_country_flag = saadabad_accept_flag }
			}
			diplomatic_relation = {
				country = TUR
				relation = non_aggression_pact
				active = yes
			}
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = TUR modifier = expand_the_sadabat_pact }
			add_ai_strategy = {
				type = antagonize
				id = "TUR"
				value = -75
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { tag = PER }
				PER = { has_country_flag = saadabad_accept_flag }
			}
			diplomatic_relation = {
				country = PER
				relation = non_aggression_pact
				active = yes
			}
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = PER modifier = expand_the_sadabat_pact }
			add_ai_strategy = {
				type = antagonize
				id = "PER"
				value = -75
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { tag = IRQ }
				IRQ = { has_country_flag = saadabad_accept_flag }
			}
			diplomatic_relation = {
				country = IRQ
				relation = non_aggression_pact
				active = yes
			}
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = IRQ modifier = expand_the_sadabat_pact }
			add_ai_strategy = {
				type = antagonize
				id = "IRQ"
				value = -75
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { tag = AFG }
				AFG = { has_country_flag = saadabad_accept_flag }
			}
			diplomatic_relation = {
				country = AFG
				relation = non_aggression_pact
				active = yes
			}
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = AFG modifier = expand_the_sadabat_pact }
			add_ai_strategy = {
				type = antagonize
				id = "AFG"
				value = -75
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { tag = EGY }
				EGY = { has_country_flag = saadabad_accept_flag }
			}
			diplomatic_relation = {
				country = EGY
				relation = non_aggression_pact
				active = yes
			}
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = EGY modifier = expand_the_sadabat_pact }
			add_ai_strategy = {
				type = antagonize
				id = "EGY"
				value = -75
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { tag = SYR }
				SYR = { has_country_flag = saadabad_accept_flag }
			}
			diplomatic_relation = {
				country = SYR
				relation = non_aggression_pact
				active = yes
			}
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = SYR modifier = expand_the_sadabat_pact }
			add_ai_strategy = {
				type = antagonize
				id = "SYR"
				value = -75
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { tag = BPL }
				BPL = { has_country_flag = saadabad_accept_flag }
			}
			diplomatic_relation = {
				country = BPL
				relation = non_aggression_pact
				active = yes
			}
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = BPL modifier = expand_the_sadabat_pact }
			add_ai_strategy = {
				type = antagonize
				id = "BPL"
				value = -75
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = PER
				IRQ = { has_country_flag = saadabad_accept_flag }
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_owned_by = PER
					is_claimed_by = IRQ
				}
				IRQ = { remove_state_claim = PREV }
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_owned_by = IRQ
					is_claimed_by = PER
				}
				PER = { remove_state_claim = PREV }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = IRQ
				PER = { has_country_flag = saadabad_accept_flag }
			}
			effect_tooltip = {
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						is_owned_by = PER
						is_claimed_by = IRQ
					}
					IRQ = { remove_state_claim = PREV }
				}
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						is_owned_by = IRQ
						is_claimed_by = PER
					}
					PER = { remove_state_claim = PREV }
				}
			}
		}
		#Новый лидер пакта
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					TUR = { NOT = { has_country_flag = saadabad_accept_flag } }
					PER = { NOT = { has_country_flag = saadabad_accept_flag } }
					AFG = { NOT = { has_country_flag = saadabad_accept_flag } }
					IRQ = { NOT = { has_country_flag = saadabad_accept_flag } }
					BPL = { NOT = { has_country_flag = saadabad_accept_flag } }
					EGY = { NOT = { has_country_flag = saadabad_accept_flag } }
					NOT = { any_other_country = { has_country_flag = new_saadabad_creator_flag } }
					any_other_country = { has_country_flag = saadabad_accept_flag }
				}
				random_country = {
					limit = {
						has_country_flag = saadabad_accept_flag
						is_in_faction = no
					}
					set_country_flag = new_saadabad_creator_flag
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

			}
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = { is_core_of = PAK }
			remove_claim_by = ROOT
		}
		
		TUR = {
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = var:current_party_ideology_group
				popularity = -0.06
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = NWturkey.55.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 60
			modifier = {
				any_of_scopes = {
					array = global.majors
					has_war_with = TUR
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}
	}
}

#Автоивент на начало войнушки
country_event = {
	id = NWturkey.57
	fire_only_once = yes
	hidden = yes
	
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NWturkey.57" }
	
	trigger = {
		threat > 0.499
		tag = RAJ
		RAJ = { has_war = yes }
		TUR = {
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = TUR_full_supply_pak
				has_country_flag = TUR_partial_supply_pak
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = NWturkey.57.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 75
		}
		if = {
			limit = { TUR = { has_country_flag = TUR_full_supply_pak } }
			PAK = {
				transfer_state = 443
				transfer_state = 444
				transfer_state = 445
				add_state_core = 443
				add_state_core = 444
				add_state_core = 445
			}
			PAK = { load_oob = "PAK_rebels" }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { TUR = { has_country_flag = TUR_partial_supply_pak } }
			PAK = {
				transfer_state = 443
				add_state_core = 443
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { TUR = { is_faction_leader = yes } }
			PAK = {
				add_ai_strategy = {
					type = befriend
					id = "TUR"			
					value = 200
				}
				add_ai_strategy = {
					type = alliance
					id = "TUR"			
					value = 200
				}
			}
			TUR = { add_to_faction = PAK }
		}
		if = { 
			limit = { TUR = { is_faction_leader = no } }
			PAK = { set_country_flag = pakistan_eng_peace_flag }
			if = {
				limit = { RAJ = { is_subject_of = ENG } }
				ENG = { set_country_flag = eng_pakistan_peace_flag_2 }
			}
			else = {
				RAJ = { set_country_flag = eng_pakistan_peace_flag_2 }
			}
		}
		RAJ = {
			declare_war_on = {
				target = PAK
				type = annex_everything
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { RAJ = { has_civil_war = yes } }
			random_country = {
				limit = { 
					original_tag = RAJ
					NOT = { tag = RAJ }
				}
				declare_war_on = {
					target = PAK
					type = annex_everything
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
}

#Пульсар. Проверка лидера
country_event = {
	id = NWturkey.68
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hidden = yes
	
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NWturkey.68" }
	
	option = {
		name = NWturkey.68.a
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					var = GER.influence
					value = 26
					compare = greater_than_or_equals
				}
			}
			clear_variable = ENG.influence
			clear_variable = GER.influence
			clear_variable = ENG.discontent
			clear_variable = GER.discontent
			complete_national_focus = TUR_alliance_with_germany
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					var = ENG.influence
					value = 26
					compare = greater_than_or_equals
				}
			}
			clear_variable = ENG.influence
			clear_variable = GER.influence
			clear_variable = ENG.discontent
			clear_variable = GER.discontent
			complete_national_focus = TUR_alliance_with_britain
		}
	}
}

						has_global_flag = NW_TUR_OLD_FOCUS_TREE
						NOT = { has_completed_focus = TUR_getting_rid_left }
					}
					AND = {
						NOT = { has_global_flag = NW_TUR_OLD_FOCUS_TREE }
						NOT = { has_completed_focus = TUR_start_fighting_left_wing_elements }
					}
				}
			}
			country_event = { id = NWturkey.70 }
		}
	}
}

		#	remove_ideas_with_trait = { fascist_demagogue }
		#}
	}
	option = {

		}
		add_stability = -0.05
		add_war_support = 0.02
		add_political_power = 50
		create_country_leader = {
			name = "Alparslan Türkeş"
			desc = "POLITICS_ALPARSLAN_TURKES_DESC"
			picture = "gfx/leaders/TUR/Portrait_Alparslan_Turkes.dds"

				anti_communist
				enemy_of_ussr
				supporter_nationalist_dictatorship

				elections_allowed = no
			}
		}
	}

					has_country_flag = NW_TUR_AI_NEUTRAL_ALTERNATE
					has_country_flag = NW_TUR_AI_DEMOCRATIC
					has_country_flag = NW_TUR_AI_FASCIST
					has_country_flag = NW_TUR_AI_TROZKIST
					has_country_flag = NW_TUR_AI_DEMOCRATIC_ALTERNATE
					has_country_flag = NW_TUR_AI_MONARCHY
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 500
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = NW_TUR_AI_COMMUNIST
					has_country_flag = NW_TUR_AI_COMMUNIST_ALTERNATE
				}
			}
		}
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event choosen NWturkey.71d"
		add_stability = -0.1
		add_war_support = -0.05
		
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = NW_new_turkey.158 days = 15 random_days = 5 } #Коммунистический переворот
		}
	}
	
	#Никого не сажать
	option = {
		name = NWturkey.71.e
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = NW_TUR_AI_NEUTRAL
					has_country_flag = NW_TUR_AI_NEUTRAL_ALTERNATE
					has_country_flag = NW_TUR_AI_DEMOCRATIC
					has_country_flag = NW_TUR_AI_FASCIST
					has_country_flag = NW_TUR_AI_TROZKIST
					has_country_flag = NW_TUR_AI_COMMUNIST
					has_country_flag = NW_TUR_AI_COMMUNIST_ALTERNATE
					has_country_flag = NW_TUR_AI_DEMOCRATIC_ALTERNATE
					has_country_flag = NW_TUR_AI_MONARCHY
				}
			}
		}
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event choosen NWturkey.71e"
		add_political_power = 50
		add_stability = -0.05
		
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = kurd_revolt_flag
						has_country_flag = kurd_revolt_over_flag
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = NWturkey.41 days = 25 }
			}
			set_global_flag = TUR_total_civil_war_flag
			set_variable = { civil_war_size = 1 }
			set_variable = { civil_war_side = 1 }
			if = {
				limit = { 
					trozkism > 0.05
				}
				add_to_variable = { civil_war_side = 1 }
				country_event = { id = NW_new_turkey.160 days = 7 random_days = 3 }
				set_global_flag = TTCW_trozkism_flag
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					set_temp_variable = { TTCW_monarchy_var = party_popularity@democratic }
					add_to_temp_variable = { TTCW_monarchy_var = party_popularity@monarchy }
					check_variable = { TTCW_monarchy_var > 0.05 }
				}
				add_to_variable = { civil_war_side = 1 }
				country_event = { id = NW_new_turkey.161 days = 8 random_days = 3 }
				set_global_flag = TTCW_monarchy_flag
			}
			if = {
				limit = { 
					communism > 0.05
				}
				add_to_variable = { civil_war_side = 1 }
				country_event = { id = NW_new_turkey.162 days = 9 random_days = 3 }
				set_global_flag = TTCW_communism_flag
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { civil_war_side > 1 }
					all_country_with_original_tag = {
						original_tag_to_check = ROOT
						NOT = { has_country_leader = { character = TUR_fevzi_cakmak ruling_only = yes } }
					}
					NOT = { focus_progress = { focus = TUR_dictatorship_cakmak progress > 0 } }
				}
				add_to_variable = { civil_war_side = 1 }
				country_event = { id = NW_new_turkey.163 days = 14 }
				news_event = { id = trworldnews.149 days = 12 }
			}
			divide_variable = { civil_war_size = civil_war_side }
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = NWturkey.85
	title = NWturkey.85.t
	desc = NWturkey.85.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_rally_3
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NWturkey.85" }
	immediate = {
		set_variable = { var_tur_bp_pp = influence_army_var }
		multiply_variable = { var_tur_bp_pp = 0.025 }
		multiply_variable = { var_tur_bp_pp = 0.1 }
		set_variable = { var_tur_bp_command_power = influence_army_var }
		multiply_variable = { var_tur_bp_command_power = 0.01 }
		set_variable = { var_tur_bp_war_support = influence_army_var }
		multiply_variable = { var_tur_bp_war_support = 0.002 }
		force_update_dynamic_modifier = yes
	}
	
	option = {
		name = NWturkey.85.a
		trigger = { NOT = { has_country_leader = { character = TUR_fevzi_cakmak ruling_only = yes } } }
		add_popularity = { ideology = neutrality popularity = 0.1 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_government = neutrality
				}
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = neutrality
				elections_allowed = no
			}
		}
#		create_country_leader = {
#			name = TUR_fevzi_cakmak
#			desc = "POLITICS_FEVZI_CAKMAK_DESC"
#			picture = "gfx/leaders/TUR/portrait_tur_fevzi_cakmak.dds"
#			expire = "1965.1.1"
#			ideology = despotism
#			traits = {
#				maresal
#				national_leader
#			}
#		}
		add_country_leader_role = {
			character = TUR_fevzi_cakmak
			promote_leader = yes
			country_leader = {
				desc = "POLITICS_FEVZI_CAKMAK_DESC"
				ideology = despotism
				expire = "1965.1.1.1"
				traits = { maresal national_leader }
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = NWturkey.85.b
		trigger = { has_country_leader = { character = TUR_fevzi_cakmak ruling_only = yes } }
		set_country_leader_portrait = {
			portrait = "GFX_portrait_tur_fevzi_cakmak"
		}
	}
}

#СССР вмешивается в гражданскую войну!
country_event = {
	id = NWturkey.89
	title = NWturkey.89.t
	desc = NWturkey.89.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_rally_3
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NWturkey.89" }

	option = {
		name = NWturkey.89.a
		effect_tooltip = {
			SOV = { add_ideas = TUR_resistance_to_invasion_of_ussr }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_template = "Turkish Militia" }
			}
			division_template = {
				name = "Turkish Militia"
				is_locked = yes
				regiments = {
					infantry = { x = 0 y = 0 }
					infantry = { x = 0 y = 1 }
					infantry = { x = 1 y = 0 }
					infantry = { x = 1 y = 1 }
				}
			}
		}
		random_controlled_state = {
			limit = { is_in_home_area = yes }
			create_unit = {
				division = "name = \"Turkish Militia\" division_template = \"Turkish Militia\" start_experience_factor = 0.1"
				owner = PREV
				count = 5
				allow_spawning_on_enemy_provs = yes
			}
		}
		add_ai_strategy = {
			type = contain
			id = FROM
			value = 200
		}
		add_ai_strategy = {
			type = antagonize
			id = FROM
			value = 400
		}
		add_ai_strategy = {
			type = alliance
			id = FROM
			value = -1000
		}
		add_ai_strategy = {
			type = befriend
			id = FROM
			value = -200
		}
	}
}



#ТЕСТ ГВ
country_event = {
	id = NWturkey.999
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hidden = yes
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NWturkey.999" }

	option = {
		name = 1
		random_other_country = {
			limit = {
				original_tag = TUR
				has_completed_focus = TUR_soviet_support
			}
			SOV = {
				add_named_threat = { threat = 5 name = TUR_intervention_in_TCW }
				set_country_flag = TUR_intervention_in_TCW_flag
				add_ideas = TUR_resistance_to_invasion_of_ussr
				add_ai_strategy = {
					type = protect
					id = PREV
					value = 100
				}
				add_ai_strategy = {
					type = support
					id = PREV
					value = 100
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_template = "Turkish Militia" }
			}
			division_template = {
				name = "Turkish Militia"
				is_locked = yes
				regiments = {
					infantry = { x = 0 y = 0 }
					infantry = { x = 0 y = 1 }
					infantry = { x = 1 y = 0 }
					infantry = { x = 1 y = 1 }
				}
			}
		}
		random_controlled_state = {
			limit = { is_in_home_area = yes }
			create_unit = {
				division = "name = \"Turkish Militia\" division_template = \"Turkish Militia\" start_experience_factor = 0.1"
				owner = PREV
				count = 5
				allow_spawning_on_enemy_provs = yes
			}
		}
		add_ai_strategy = {
			type = contain
			id = SOV
			value = 200
		}
		add_ai_strategy = {
			type = antagonize
			id = SOV
			value = 400
		}
		add_ai_strategy = {
			type = alliance
			id = SOV
			value = -1000
		}
		add_ai_strategy = {
			type = befriend
			id = SOV
			value = -200
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = 2
		delete_unit_template_and_units = {
			division_template = "Turkish Militia 2"
			disband = yes
		}
		delete_unit_template_and_units = {
			division_template = "Turkish Militia 3"
			disband = yes
		}
	}
}

#Турция хочет взять кредит \\ ENG \ SOV \ GER
country_event = {
	id = NW_new_turkey.1
	title = NW_new_turkey.1.t
	desc = NW_new_turkey.1.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_rally_3
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_new_turkey.1" }
	
	option = {
		name = NW_new_turkey.1.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 90
		}
		random_owned_controlled_state = {
			limit = {
				industrial_complex > 1
			}
			remove_building = {
				type = industrial_complex
				level = 1
			}
		}
		random_owned_controlled_state = {
			limit = {
				industrial_complex > 1
			}
			remove_building = {
				type = industrial_complex
				level = 1
			}
		}
		random_owned_controlled_state = {
			limit = {
				industrial_complex > 0
			}
			remove_building = {
				type = industrial_complex
				level = 1
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = ROOT modifier = TUR_take_credit }
			hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = NW_new_turkey.2 days = 1 } }
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = NW_new_turkey_1a_tt
	}
	option = {
		name = NW_new_turkey.1.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 5
				has_war = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 10
				any_enemy_country = {
					any_controlled_state = { is_core_of = ROOT }
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = { FROM = { country_event = { id = NW_new_turkey.3 days = 1 } } }
	}
}

	id = NW_new_turkey.2
	title = NW_new_turkey.2.t
	desc = NW_new_turkey.2.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_rally_3
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_new_turkey.2" }
	
	option = {
		name = NW_new_turkey.2.a
		random_owned_controlled_state = {
			limit = { 
				free_building_slots = {
					building = industrial_complex
					size > 2
					include_locked = yes
				}
			}
			add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 3
			add_building_construction = {
				type = industrial_complex
				level = 3
				instant_build = yes
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { tag = ENG } }
			add_timed_idea = { idea = TUR_debt_to_eng days = 300 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { tag = SOV } }
			add_timed_idea = { idea = TUR_debt_to_sov days = 300 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { tag = GER } }
			add_timed_idea = { idea = TUR_debt_to_ger days = 300 }
		}
	}
}

	desc = NW_new_turkey.5.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_rally_3
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_new_turkey.5" }
	
	option = {
		name = NW_new_turkey.5.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_in_faction = yes
				FROM = { is_in_faction = no }
			}
		}
		FROM = { country_event = { id = NW_new_turkey.6 days = 1 } }
		if = {
			limit = {
				country_exists = PER
				NOT = {
					original_tag = PER
					has_war_with = PER
				}
			}
			PER = { country_event = { id = NW_new_turkey.9 days = 1 } }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = NW_new_turkey.5.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 75
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					threat > 0.30
					FROM = { NOT = { has_government = neutrality } }
				}
				FROM = { alliance_strength_ratio > 1 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_in_faction = yes
				FROM = { is_in_faction = no }
			}
		}
		FROM = { country_event = { id = NW_new_turkey.10 days = 1 } }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = NW_new_turkey.5.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					threat > 0.30
					FROM = { NOT = { has_government = neutrality } }
				}
				FROM = { alliance_strength_ratio > 1 }
			}
		}
		add_opinion_modifier = { target = FROM modifier = diplomatic_affront }
		FROM = {
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = ROOT modifier = diplomatic_affront }
			add_ai_strategy = {
				type = contain
				id = ROOT
				value = 200
			}
		}
		add_ai_strategy = {
			type = contain
			id = FROM
			value = 200
		}
	}
}

			}
		}

		}

			type = conquer
			id = FROM

		}

			id = FROM

country_event = {
	id = NW_new_turkey.10
	title = NW_new_turkey.10.t
	desc = NW_new_turkey.10.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_rally_3
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_new_turkey.10" }
	
	option = {
		name = NW_new_turkey.10.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { owns_state = 676 } }
			676 = { set_demilitarized_zone = yes }
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_owned_by = FROM
				OR = {
					state = 676
					state = 962
				}
			}
			remove_core_of = FROM
			ROOT = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}
		give_guarantee = FROM
		diplomatic_relation = {
			country = FROM
			relation = non_aggression_pact
			active = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					original_tag = IRQ
					has_focus_tree = nw_iraq_focus
					NOT = { has_completed_focus = IRQ_nationalization_of_oil_fields }
				}
			}
			country_event = { id = NW_new_turkey.7 days = 1 }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = NW_new_turkey.10.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}
		FROM = { country_event = { id = NW_new_turkey.11 days = 1 } }
	}
}

#Турецкий ультиматум // ITA
country_event = {
	id = NW_new_turkey.14
	title = NW_new_turkey.14.t
	desc = NW_new_turkey.14.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_rally_3
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_new_turkey.14" }
	
	option = {
		name = NW_new_turkey.14.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
		}
		every_other_country = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					tag = FROM
					is_in_faction_with = FROM
				}
			}
			ROOT = {
				diplomatic_relation = {
					country = PREV
					relation = non_aggression_pact
					active = yes
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { YUG = { is_in_faction_with = FROM } }
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_owned_by = ROOT
					OR = {
						state = 163
						state = 736
						state = 823
						state = 824
					}
				}
				add_core_of = YUG
				YUG = { transfer_state = PREV }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 164 = { is_owned_by = ROOT } }
			164 = {
				add_core_of = FROM
				FROM = { transfer_state = PREV }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { ALB = { is_subject_of = ROOT } }
			set_autonomy = {
				target = ALB
				autonomy_state = autonomy_free
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = NW_new_turkey.14.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 90
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				FROM = { alliance_strength_ratio > 1 }
			}
		}
		FROM = { country_event = { id = nw_greece.68 days = 1 } }
	}
}

#Ультиматум балканских стран \\ BUL
country_event = {
	id = NW_new_turkey.15
	title = NW_new_turkey.15.t
	desc = NW_new_turkey.15.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_rally_3
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_new_turkey.15" }
	
	option = {
		name = NW_new_turkey.15.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}
		add_ideas = TUR_turkish_bulgarian_agreement
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction = yes
				is_faction_leader = yes
			}
			every_other_country = {
				limit = { is_in_faction_with = ROOT }
				ROOT = {
					add_ai_strategy = {
						type = alliance
						id = PREV
						value = -600
					}
				}
			}
			leave_faction = yes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction = yes
			}
			random_other_country = {
				limit = {
					is_in_faction_with = ROOT
					is_faction_leader = yes
				}
				ROOT = {
					add_ai_strategy = {
						type = alliance
						id = PREV
						value = -600
					}
				}
			}
			leave_faction = yes
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					OR = {
						tag = FROM
						is_in_faction_with = FROM
					}
				}
				OR = {
					is_claimed_by = ROOT
					is_core_of = ROOT
				}
			}
			remove_claim_by = ROOT
			remove_core_of = ROOT
		}
		every_other_country = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					tag = FROM
					is_in_faction_with = FROM
				}
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_owned_by = ROOT
					is_claimed_by = PREV
					NOT = { is_owned_by = PREV }
				}
				PREV = { transfer_state = PREV }
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_owned_by = ROOT
					is_core_of = PREV
					NOT = { is_owned_by = PREV }
				}
				PREV = { transfer_state = PREV }
			}
		}
		48 = { owner = { give_resource_rights = { receiver = FROM state = 48 } } }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = NW_new_turkey.15.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}
		FROM = { country_event = { id = NW_new_turkey.16 days = 1 } }
	}
}

	desc = NW_new_turkey.36.desc

	option = {
		name = NW_new_turkey.36.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}
		add_political_power = 15
	}
	
	option = {
		name = NW_new_turkey.36.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
		}
		trigger = { NOT = { check_variable = { TUR_loyalty_communists_var < 0 } } }
		set_country_flag = NW_new_turkey_36b_flag
		add_political_power = -30
		add_stability = 0.05
		add_timed_idea = { idea = TUR_legalizing_movement_of_personnel days = 60 }
		set_party_name = { ideology = communism name = TUR_movement_of_personnel_party long_name = TUR_movement_of_personnel_party }
		TUR_sevket_aydemir = {
			promote_character = yes
	    }
		if = {
			limit = { has_focus_tree = nw_turkish_focus_new }
			custom_effect_tooltip = NW_new_turkey_36b_tt
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = NW_new_turkey.36.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
		}
		trigger = { has_country_flag = NW_new_turkey_34a_flag }
		set_country_flag = NW_new_turkey_36c_flag
		add_political_power = -30
		add_stability = 0.05
		add_timed_idea = { idea = TUR_changing_ideology_of_movement_of_personnel days = 60 }
		if = {
			limit = { has_focus_tree = nw_turkish_focus_new }
			set_party_name = { ideology = trozkism name = TUR_movement_of_personnel_party long_name = TUR_movement_of_personnel_party }
			custom_effect_tooltip = NW_new_turkey_36c_tt
		}
	}
}

		}

		}

		name = NW_new_turkey.47.a

			add_opinion_modifier = { target = FROM modifier = TUR_accepted_offer_of_concessions }

				add_opinion_modifier = { target = ROOT modifier = TUR_to_support_economy }

			}
		}
		random_owned_controlled_state = {
			limit = {
				industrial_complex > 0
			}
			remove_building = {
				type = industrial_complex
				level = 1
			}
		}
		random_owned_controlled_state = {
			limit = {
				industrial_complex > 0
			}
			remove_building = {
				type = industrial_complex
				level = 1
			}
		}
		random_owned_controlled_state = {
			limit = {
				industrial_complex > 0
			}
			remove_building = {
				type = industrial_complex
				level = 1
			}
		}
		random_owned_controlled_state = {
			limit = {
				industrial_complex > 0
			}
			remove_building = {
				type = industrial_complex
				level = 1
			}

		if = {
			limit = { has_wargoal_against = FROM }

				relation = non_aggression_pact
				active = yes
			}

country_event = {
	id = NW_new_turkey.55
	title = NW_new_turkey.55.t
	desc = NW_new_turkey.55.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_rally_3
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_new_turkey.55" }
	
	option = {
		name = NW_new_turkey.55.a
		trigger = { check_variable = { structure_of_anarcho_kemalism_var < 0 } }
		set_country_flag = anarchism_left_flag
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_idea = peoples_squads
					has_idea = peoples_police
					has_idea = peoples_militia
					has_active_mission = generic_anarchism_manpower_decision
				}
			}
			activate_mission = generic_anarchism_manpower_decision
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = NW_new_turkey.55.b
		trigger = { check_variable = { structure_of_anarcho_kemalism_var = 0 } }
		set_country_flag = anarchism_left_flag
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_idea = peoples_squads
					has_idea = peoples_police
					has_idea = peoples_militia
					has_active_mission = generic_anarchism_manpower_decision
				}
			}
			activate_mission = generic_anarchism_manpower_decision
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = NW_new_turkey.55.c
		trigger = { check_variable = { structure_of_anarcho_kemalism_var > 0 } }
		set_country_flag = anarchism_right_flag
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_idea = mercenary_soldiers

			}

		}
	}

			if = {
				limit = { communism > 0.099 }
				country_event = { id = NW_new_turkey.59 days = 5 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { democratic > 0.199 }
				country_event = { id = NW_new_turkey.60 days = 10 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { fascism > 0.01 }
				country_event = { id = NW_new_turkey.61 days = 15 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = NW_new_turkey_34a_flag
					NOT = { has_completed_focus = TUR_revive_the_green_army }
				}
				country_event = { id = NW_new_turkey.62 days = 20 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = NW_new_turkey_34a_flag
					has_completed_focus = TUR_revive_the_green_army
				}
				country_event = { id = NW_new_turkey.64 days = 20 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_country_flag = TUR_liberalization_of_political_life_flag
						has_country_flag = TUR_bet_on_pan_turkist_flag
						has_country_flag = TUR_building_socialism_flag
						has_country_flag = TUR_reject_statism_flag
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = NW_new_turkey.68 days = 25 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						democratic > 0.299
						has_country_flag = TUR_return_to_islamism_flag
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = NW_new_turkey.69 days = 23 }

					has_country_flag = TUR_return_to_islamism_flag

						operative_leader_mission = counter_intelligence
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = NW_new_turkey.70 days = 25 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = TUR_return_to_islamism_flag
				}
				country_event = { id = NW_new_turkey.71 days = 40 }
			}
			country_event = { id = NW_new_turkey.73 days = 50 }
			country_event = { id = NW_new_turkey.77 days = 65 }
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = NW_new_turkey.58.a
		add_country_leader_role = {
			character = TUR_ismet_inonu
			country_leader = {
				desc = "POLITICS_ISMET_INÖNÜ_DESC"
				ideology = kemalism
				traits = {
					milli_sef
				}
				expire = "1965.1.1"
			}
			promote_leader = yes
		}

		hidden_effect = {
			news_event = { id = trworldnews.57 hours = 6 }
		}
	}

					}
				}

					}

						state = 786
						state = 1049
						state = 354
					}
				}
				else = {
					OR = {
						state = 352
						state = 350
						state = 786
						state = 355
						state = 356
						state = 347
					}
				}
				
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			random_other_country = {
				limit = {
					original_tag = ROOT
					has_government = trozkism
				}
				load_focus_tree = { tree = nw_turkish_focus_new keep_completed = no }
				TUR_focus_synchronization = yes

				owner = {
					OR = {
						original_tag = ROOT
						is_subject_of = ROOT
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						TUR = { has_completed_focus = TUR_evicting_circassians_in_eastern_anatolia }
					}
					OR = {
						state = 352
						state = 350
						state = 786
						state = 1049
						state = 354
					}
				}
				else = {

			size = 0.5

					}

						state = 350
						state = 786

						state = 347

			states_filter = {

#Правительство требует соблюдать конституцию \\ TUR
country_event = {
	id = NW_new_turkey.68
	title = NW_new_turkey.68.t
	desc = NW_new_turkey.68.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_rally_3
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_new_turkey.68" }

	option = {
		name = NW_new_turkey.68.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = TUR_reject_statism_flag }
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = anarchism
				elections_allowed = no
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = TUR_liberalization_of_political_life_flag }
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = democratic
				elections_allowed = yes
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = TUR_bet_on_pan_turkist_flag }
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = fascism
				elections_allowed = no
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = TUR_building_socialism_flag }
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = communism
				elections_allowed = no
			}
		}
		add_opinion_modifier = { target = SOV modifier = TUR_communist_party_relegated_background }
		SOV = { add_opinion_modifier = { target = ROOT modifier = TUR_communist_party_relegated_background } }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = NW_new_turkey.68.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = TUR_reject_statism_flag }
			add_stability = party_popularity@anarchism
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = TUR_liberalization_of_political_life_flag }
			add_stability = party_popularity@democratic
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = TUR_bet_on_pan_turkist_flag }
			add_stability = party_popularity@fascism
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = TUR_building_socialism_flag }
			add_stability = party_popularity@communism
		}
		add_timed_idea = { idea = TUR_government_resignation days = 30 }
	}
}

						division = "name = \"4. Rebels\" division_template = \"Rebels\" start_experience_factor = 0.2"
						owner = PREV
					}
					create_unit = {
						division = "name = \"5. Rebels\" division_template = \"Rebels\" start_experience_factor = 0.2"
						owner = PREV
					}
				}
			}
		}
		random_other_country = {
			limit = {
				original_tag = ROOT
				has_government = democratic
			}
			change_tag_from = ROOT
			hidden_effect = {
				load_focus_tree = { tree = nw_turkish_focus_new keep_completed = no }
				TUR_focus_synchronization = yes
				unlock_national_focus = TUR_correction_constitution
				unlock_national_focus = TUR_call_for_creation_of_opposition_parties
				unlock_national_focus = TUR_spend_change_of_government
				complete_national_focus = TUR_liberalization_of_political_life
				complete_national_focus = TUR_political_transformation
			}

#Пульсар. Февзи Чакмак поддерживает правительство // TUR
country_event = {
	id = NW_new_turkey.73
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hidden = yes
	
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_new_turkey.73" }
	
	option = {
		name = NW_new_turkey.73.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_civil_war = no
				NOT = {
					any_army_leader = {
						has_nationality = ROOT
						has_id = 1800
					}
				}
				OR = {
					has_government = neutrality
					has_government = democratic
				}
			}
			country_event = { id = NW_new_turkey.74 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_civil_war = no
					OR = {
						has_government = communism
						has_government = fascism
						has_government = anarchism
					}
				}
			}
			country_event = { id = NW_new_turkey.75 }
		}
	}
}

			}

	}
	
	option = {

			factor = 50

				original_tag = TUR
				copy_tag = TUR
				set_country_flag = TUR_trk
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = TUR
				}
				add_core_of = TRK
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						state = 49
						state = 343
						state = 349
						state = 348
						state = 345
					}
				}
				TRK = { transfer_state = PREV }
			}
			ROOT = {
				TUR_fevzi_cakmak = { set_nationality = TRK }
			}
			TRK = {
				set_popularities = {
					neutrality = 5
					fascism = 95
				}
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = fascism
					elections_allowed = no
				}
				add_ideas = generic_civil_war
				set_cosmetic_tag = TUR_dictatorship_tag
#				create_country_leader = {
#					name = TUR_fevzi_cakmak
#					desc = "POLITICS_FEVZI_CAKMAK_DESC"
#					picture = "gfx/leaders/TUR/portrait_tur_fevzi_cakmak.dds"
#					expire = "1965.1.1"
#					ideology = nationalism_ideology
#					traits = { maresal }
#				}
				add_country_leader_role = {
					character = TUR_fevzi_cakmak
					promote_leader = yes
					country_leader = {
						desc = "POLITICS_FEVZI_CAKMAK_DESC"
						ideology = nationalism_ideology

						traits = { maresal }
					}
				}

				load_focus_tree = { tree = nw_turkish_focus_new keep_completed = no }
				TUR_focus_synchronization = yes
				unlock_national_focus = TUR_correction_constitution
				unlock_national_focus = TUR_call_for_creation_of_opposition_parties
				unlock_national_focus = TUR_spend_change_of_government
				complete_national_focus = TUR_bet_on_nationalism
				complete_national_focus = TUR_carry_out_militarization_of_society
				complete_national_focus = TUR_political_transformation
				declare_war_on = {
					target = ROOT
					type = civil_war
				}
				add_civil_war_target = ROOT
			}
			news_event = { id = trworldnews.56 hours = 6 }

				type = alliance

				value = -200
			}
		}
		diplomatic_relation = { country = FROM relation = guarantee active = no }

		}

		FROM = { country_event = { id = NW_new_turkey.112 days = 1 } }
		custom_effect_tooltip = NW_new_turkey_111b_tt
	}
	
	option = {
		name = NW_new_turkey.111.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { is_in_faction_with = ROOT } }
			add_ai_strategy = {
				type = alliance
				id = FROM
				value = -200
			}
			FROM = {
				leave_faction = yes
				add_ai_strategy = {
					type = alliance
					id = ROOT
					value = -200
				}
			}
		}
		create_wargoal = {
			type = take_state_focus
			target = FROM
			generator = { 1026 }
		}
		add_ai_strategy = {
			type = antagonize
			id = FROM
			value = 200
		}
		add_ai_strategy = {
			type = conquer
			id = FROM
			value = 200
		}

				check_variable = { TUR_loyalty_islamists_var < 1 }

				check_variable = { TUR_loyalty_communists_var < 0 }
				check_variable = { TUR_loyalty_chakmak_var < 0 }
				check_variable = { TUR_loyalty_inenu_var < 0 }
			}
			country_event = { id = NW_new_turkey.136 }
		}
	}
}

	id = NW_new_turkey.140
	title = NW_new_turkey.140.t
	desc = NW_new_turkey.140.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_rally_3
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_new_turkey.140" }

	option = {
		name = NW_new_turkey.140.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 99
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				FROM = { has_government = trozkism }
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			add_ideas = TUR_popes_call_for_unity
		}
		add_ai_strategy = {
			type = alliance
			id = FROM
			value = 200
		}
		add_named_threat = { threat = -1 name = TUR_popes_call_for_unity }
		every_other_country = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					original_tag = ITA
					original_tag = FRA
					original_tag = SPR
					original_tag = POR
					original_tag = BEL
					original_tag = GER
					original_tag = LUX
					original_tag = HOL
					original_tag = IRE
					original_tag = AUS
					original_tag = HUN
					original_tag = CRO
					original_tag = SLV
					original_tag = POL
					original_tag = EST
					original_tag = LIT
					original_tag = LAT
					original_tag = CZE
					original_tag = SLO
				}
				NOT = {
					has_government = communism
					has_government = trozkism
					has_government = anarchism
					has_government = technocracy
				}
			}
			country_event = { id = NW_new_turkey.142 hours = 6 }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = NW_new_turkey.140.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
		FROM = { country_event = { id = NW_new_turkey.141 hours = 6 } }
	}

country_event = {
	id = NW_new_turkey.142
	title = NW_new_turkey.142.t
	desc = NW_new_turkey.142.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_rally_3
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_new_turkey.142" }

	option = {
		name = NW_new_turkey.142.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}
		add_opinion_modifier = { target = FROM modifier = TUR_ignore_pope_op }
		FROM = { add_opinion_modifier = { target = ROOT modifier = TUR_ignore_pope_op } }
		set_temp_variable = { temp1 = party_popularity@fascism }
		add_to_temp_variable = { temp1 = party_popularity@monarchy }
		add_to_temp_variable = { temp1 = party_popularity@neutrality }
		multiply_temp_variable = { temp1 = -0.5 }
		add_stability = temp1
	}
	
	option = {
		name = NW_new_turkey.142.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_government = fascism
					has_government = monarchy
					has_government = neutrality
				}
			}
		}
		add_to_temp_variable = { temp2 = party_popularity@democratic }
		multiply_temp_variable = { temp2 = -0.5 }
		add_stability = temp2
		FROM.FROM = {
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = ROOT modifier = TUR_supported_unity_people_of_scripture_op }
			diplomatic_relation = {
				country = ROOT
				relation = non_aggression_pact
				active = yes
			}
			ROOT = { add_opinion_modifier = { target = PREV modifier = TUR_supported_unity_people_of_scripture_op } }
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = NW_new_turkey.147
	title = NW_new_turkey.147.t
	desc = NW_new_turkey.147.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_rally_3
	
	trigger = {
		original_tag = TUR
		has_idea = TUR_support_for_enterprises_in_western_anatolia
		has_stability > 0.599
		OR = {
			controls_state = 340
			controls_state = 339
			controls_state = 342
			controls_state = 347
			controls_state = 964
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 5
	}
	
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_new_turkey.147" }
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			random_controlled_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						state = 340
						state = 339
						state = 342
						state = 347
						state = 964
					}
				}
				save_event_target_as = NW_new_turkey_147_target
				ROOT = { goto_state = PREV }
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = NW_new_turkey.147.a
		event_target:NW_new_turkey_147_target = {
			add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
			random_list = {
				70 = {
					add_building_construction = {
						type = industrial_complex
						level = 1
						instant_build = yes
					}
				}
				20 = {
					add_building_construction = {
						type = infrastructure
						level = 1
						instant_build = yes
					}
					add_building_construction = {
						type = industrial_complex
						level = 1
						instant_build = yes
					}
				}
				10 = {
					add_building_construction = {
						type = arms_factory
						level = 1
						instant_build = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

#Ухудшение здоровья Мустафы Кемаля Ататюрка пульсар \\ TUR \ 1 января 1937 года
country_event = {
	id = NW_new_turkey.1500
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hidden = yes
	
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_new_turkey.1500" }
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_leader = {
					character = TUR_mustafa_kemal_ataturk
					ruling_only = yes 
				}  
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_country_leader_with_trait = seriously_ill } }
				country_event = { id = NW_new_turkey.150 }
				else = {
					country_event = { id = NW_new_turkey.151 }
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

	desc = NW_new_turkey.150.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_rally_3
	is_triggered_only = yes

#Духовенство призывает к поддержке президента \\ TUR
country_event = {
	id = NW_new_turkey.152
	title = NW_new_turkey.152.t
	desc = NW_new_turkey.152.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_rally_3
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	trigger = {
		tag = TUR
		has_country_leader = {
			character = TUR_mustafa_kemal_ataturk
			ruling_only = yes 
		}  
		has_completed_focus = TUR_return_to_islamism
		OR = {
			has_completed_focus = TUR_return_to_islamism
			AND = {
				has_completed_focus = TUR_nationalism
				NOT = { has_completed_focus = TUR_secularism }
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { t1 = party_popularity@democratic }
		add_to_temp_variable = { t1 = party_popularity@monarchy }
		check_variable = { var = t1 value = 0.05 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 5
	}
	
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_new_turkey.152" }

	option = {
		name = NW_new_turkey.152.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_focus_tree = nw_turkish_focus } }
			add_political_power = 100
		}
		add_stability = 0.05
		add_popularity = { ideology = democratic popularity = 0.1 }
		add_popularity = { ideology = monarchy popularity = 0.1 }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = NW_new_turkey.152.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_focus_tree = nw_turkish_focus } }
			add_political_power = 50
		}
		add_popularity = { ideology = democratic popularity = 0.05 }
		add_popularity = { ideology = monarchy popularity = 0.05 }
	}
}

				ideology = communism
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			add_ideas = generic_civil_war
			create_dynamic_country = {
				original_tag = ROOT

				add_ideas = generic_civil_war
				set_country_flag = troz_focus_block_flag
				add_popularity = {

					popularity = 1

					ruling_party = communism
					elections_allowed = no
				}
				every_state = {

					add_core_of = PREV
				}

					limit = {

							state = 353

				complete_national_focus = TUR_commust_revolt
				set_capital = { state = 341 }
				ROOT = {
					if = {
						limit = { has_government = communism }

					}
					transfer_units_fraction = {

				}
				every_other_country = {
					limit = {
						original_tag = ROOT
						NOT = { tag = ROOT }
					}
					declare_war_on = {
						target = PREV
						type = civil_war
					}

					}
					declare_war_on = {

					}

						}
					}
				}
				random_controlled_state = {

					create_unit = {

country_event = {
	id = NW_new_turkey.159
	title = NW_new_turkey.159.t
	desc = NW_new_turkey.159.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_rally_3
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_new_turkey.159" }

	option = {
		name = NW_new_turkey.67.a
		effect_tooltip = {
			start_civil_war = {
				ideology = communism
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			add_ideas = generic_civil_war
			create_dynamic_country = {
				original_tag = ROOT
				copy_tag = ROOT
				add_ideas = generic_civil_war
				set_country_flag = troz_focus_block_flag
				if = {
					limit = { ROOT = { has_government = communism } }
					set_country_flag = same_ideology_civil_war_flag
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = neutrality
					popularity = 1
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = democratic
					popularity = 0.25
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = trozkism
					popularity = 0.1
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = fascism
					popularity = 0.1
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = monarchy
					popularity = 0.05
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = communism
					popularity = 0.2
				}
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = communism
					elections_allowed = no
				}
				every_state = {
					limit = { is_core_of = ROOT }
					add_core_of = PREV
				}
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							state = 1128
							state = 353
							AND = {
								NOT = { has_global_flag = TUR_total_civil_war_flag }
								state = 353
							}
						}
						controller = {
							OR = {
								original_tag = ROOT
								original_tag = KRD
							}
						}
					}
					PREV = { transfer_state = PREV }
				}
				load_focus_tree = { tree = nw_turkish_focus keep_completed = no }
				TUR_focus_synchronization = yes
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_idea = TUR_backwardness_of_army_1 } }
					add_ideas = TUR_backwardness_of_army_1
				}
				unlock_national_focus = TUR_commust_revolt
				complete_national_focus = TUR_turkey_communist_party
				add_timed_idea = { idea = TUR_begin_building_of_socialism_idea days = 160 }
				set_party_name = { ideology = communism name = TUR_communism_party long_name = TUR_communism_party_long }
				set_cosmetic_tag = TUR_prosoviet_tag
				ROOT = {
					if = {
						limit = { has_government = communism }
						set_country_flag = same_ideology_civil_war_flag
					}
					transfer_units_fraction = {
						target = PREV
						size = 0.3
						stockpile_ratio = 0.3
						army_ratio = 0.3
						navy_ratio = 0.3
						air_ratio = 0.3
					}
					declare_war_on = {
						target = PREV
						type = civil_war
					}
					add_civil_war_target = PREV
				}
				every_other_country = {
					limit = {
						original_tag = ROOT
						NOT = { tag = ROOT }
					}
					declare_war_on = {
						target = PREV
						type = civil_war
					}
					add_civil_war_target = PREV
					PREV = { add_civil_war_target = PREV }
				}
				add_civil_war_target = ROOT
				if = {
					limit = {
						ROOT = { has_war_with = KRD }
					}
					declare_war_on = {
						target = KRD
						type = annex_everything
					}
				}
				every_enemy_country = {
					every_state = {

							NOT = { is_fully_controlled_by = PREV }

								tag = PREV.PREV
							}

						is_locked = yes

							infantry = { x = 0 y = 1 }

country_event = {
	id = NW_new_turkey.160
	title = NW_new_turkey.67.t
	desc = NW_new_turkey.67.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_tur_machine_gunners
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_new_turkey.160" }

	option = {
		name = NW_new_turkey.67.a
		effect_tooltip = {
			start_civil_war = {
				ideology = trozkism
			}
		}
		every_other_country = {
			limit = {
				has_guaranteed = ROOT
			}
			diplomatic_relation = {
				country = ROOT
				relation = guarantee
				active = no
			}
			ROOT = {
				diplomatic_relation = {
					country = PREV
					relation = guarantee
					active = no
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			add_ideas = generic_civil_war
			create_dynamic_country = {
				original_tag = ROOT
				copy_tag = ROOT
				add_ideas = generic_civil_war
				set_country_flag = troz_focus_block_flag
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = trozkism
					name = TUR_trozkism_green_army_party
					long_name = TUR_trozkism_party_green_army_long
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = neutrality
					popularity = 1
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = democratic
					popularity = 0.25
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = communism
					popularity = 0.1
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = fascism
					popularity = 0.1
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = monarchy

				}

							state = 355
							state = 348
							state = 349
						}
						controller = {
							OR = {
								original_tag = ROOT
								original_tag = KRD
							}
						}
					}
					PREV = { transfer_state = PREV }
				}
				load_focus_tree = { tree = nw_turkish_focus keep_completed = no }
				TUR_focus_synchronization = yes
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_idea = TUR_backwardness_of_army_1 } }
					add_ideas = TUR_backwardness_of_army_1
				}
				complete_national_focus = TUR_etchem_circassian_coup
				ROOT = {
					transfer_units_fraction = {
						target = PREV
						size = civil_war_size
						stockpile_ratio = civil_war_size
						army_ratio = civil_war_size
						navy_ratio = civil_war_size
						air_ratio = civil_war_size
					}
					declare_war_on = {
						target = PREV
						type = civil_war
					}
					add_civil_war_target = PREV
					set_variable = { civil_war_size = 1 }
					add_to_variable = { civil_war_side = -1 }
					divide_variable = { civil_war_size = civil_war_side }
				}
				every_other_country = {
					limit = {
						original_tag = ROOT
						NOT = { tag = ROOT }
					}
					declare_war_on = {
						target = PREV
						type = civil_war
					}
					add_civil_war_target = PREV

				}

					limit = {

					}
					declare_war_on = {
						target = KRD
						type = annex_everything
					}
				}
				every_enemy_country = {
					every_state = {
						limit = {
							NOT = { is_fully_controlled_by = PREV }
							controller = {
								tag = PREV.PREV
							}
						}
						teleport_armies = {
							limit = {
								tag = PREV
							}
