						infantry = { x = 0 y = 1 }
						infantry = { x = 1 y = 0 }
						infantry = { x = 1 y = 1 }
					}
				}
			}
			random_controlled_state = {
				limit = { is_in_home_area = yes }
				create_unit = {
					division = "name = \"Turkish Militia\" division_template = \"Turkish Militia\" start_experience_factor = 0.1"
					owner = PREV
					count = 5
					allow_spawning_on_enemy_provs = yes
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_in_faction = yes
					is_faction_leader = no
				}
				leave_faction = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = { is_faction_leader = yes }
				dismantle_faction = yes
			}
		}
	}

country_event = {
	id = NW_new_turkey.161
	title = NW_new_turkey.161.t
	desc = NW_new_turkey.161.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_tur_sultan_and_pashas
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_new_turkey.161" }

	option = {
		name = NW_new_turkey.72.a
		effect_tooltip = {
			start_civil_war = {
				ideology = monarchy
			}
		}
		every_other_country = {
			limit = {
				has_guaranteed = ROOT
			}
			diplomatic_relation = {
				country = ROOT
				relation = guarantee
				active = no
			}
			ROOT = {
				diplomatic_relation = {
					country = PREV
					relation = guarantee
					active = no
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			add_ideas = generic_civil_war
			create_dynamic_country = {
				original_tag = ROOT
				copy_tag = ROOT
				add_ideas = generic_civil_war
				set_capital = { state =  341 }
				set_country_flag = monarch_focus_block_flag
				set_party_name = { ideology = monarchy name = TUR_monarchy_force_of_order_party long_name = TUR_monarchy_force_of_order_party }
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = neutrality
					popularity = 1
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = democratic
					popularity = 0.2
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = fascism
					popularity = 0.3
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = trozkism
					popularity = 0.05
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = communism
					popularity = 0.05
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = monarchy
					popularity = 0.22
				}
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = monarchy
					elections_allowed = no
				}
				every_state = {
					limit = { is_core_of = ROOT }
					add_core_of = PREV
				}
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							state = 345
							state = 346
							state = 344
						}
						controller = {
							OR = {
								original_tag = ROOT
								original_tag = KRD
							}
						}
					}
					PREV = { transfer_state = PREV }
				}
				load_focus_tree = { tree = nw_turkish_focus keep_completed = no }
				TUR_focus_synchronization = yes
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_idea = TUR_backwardness_of_army_1 } }
					add_ideas = TUR_backwardness_of_army_1
				}
				complete_national_focus = TUR_force_of_order
				every_other_country = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							has_character = TUR_suleyman_sefik_pasha
							has_character = TUR_kazim_karabekir
							has_character = TUR_nuri_killigil
							has_character = TUR_riza_nur
							has_character = TUR_fakhri_pasha
							has_character = TUR_ali_ihsan_sabis
							has_character = TUR_halil_kut
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = { has_character = TUR_suleyman_sefik_pasha }
						TUR_suleyman_sefik_pasha = { set_nationality = PREV.PREV }
					}
					if = {
						limit = { has_character = TUR_kazim_karabekir }
						TUR_kazim_karabekir = { 
						    set_nationality = PREV.PREV 
						    promote_character = yes
						}	
					}
					if = {
						limit = { has_character = TUR_nuri_killigil }
						TUR_nuri_killigil = { set_nationality = PREV.PREV }
					}
					if = {
						limit = { has_character = TUR_riza_nur }
						TUR_riza_nur = { set_nationality = PREV.PREV }
					}
					if = {
						limit = { has_character = TUR_fakhri_pasha }
						TUR_fakhri_pasha = { set_nationality = PREV.PREV }
					}
					if = {
						limit = { has_character = TUR_ali_ihsan_sabis }
						TUR_ali_ihsan_sabis = { set_nationality = PREV.PREV }
					}
					if = {
						limit = { has_character = TUR_halil_kut }
						TUR_halil_kut = { set_nationality = PREV.PREV }
					}
				}
				ROOT = {
					transfer_units_fraction = {
						target = PREV
						size = civil_war_size
						stockpile_ratio = civil_war_size
						army_ratio = civil_war_size
						navy_ratio = civil_war_size
						air_ratio = civil_war_size
					}
					declare_war_on = {
						target = PREV
						type = civil_war
					}
					add_civil_war_target = PREV
					set_variable = { civil_war_size = 1 }
					add_to_variable = { civil_war_side = -1 }
					divide_variable = { civil_war_size = civil_war_side }
				}
				every_other_country = {
					limit = {
						original_tag = ROOT
						NOT = { tag = ROOT }
					}
					declare_war_on = {
						target = PREV
						type = civil_war
					}
					add_civil_war_target = PREV
					PREV = { add_civil_war_target = PREV }
				}
				add_civil_war_target = ROOT
				if = {
					limit = {
						ROOT = { has_war_with = KRD }
					}
					declare_war_on = {
						target = KRD
						type = annex_everything
					}
				}
				every_enemy_country = {
					every_state = {
						limit = {
							NOT = { is_fully_controlled_by = PREV }
							controller = {
								tag = PREV.PREV
							}
						}
						teleport_armies = {
							limit = {
								tag = PREV
							}
							to_state_array = controlled_states
						}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { has_template = "Turkish Militia" }
					}
					division_template = {
						name = "Turkish Militia"
						is_locked = yes
						regiments = {
							infantry = { x = 0 y = 0 }
							infantry = { x = 0 y = 1 }
							infantry = { x = 1 y = 0 }
							infantry = { x = 1 y = 1 }
						}
					}
				}
				random_controlled_state = {
					limit = { is_in_home_area = yes }
					create_unit = {
						division = "name = \"Turkish Militia\" division_template = \"Turkish Militia\" start_experience_factor = 0.1"
						owner = PREV
						count = 10
						allow_spawning_on_enemy_provs = yes
					}
				}
			}
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_template = "Turkish Militia" }
				}
				division_template = {
					name = "Turkish Militia"
					is_locked = yes
					regiments = {
						infantry = { x = 0 y = 0 }
						infantry = { x = 0 y = 1 }
						infantry = { x = 1 y = 0 }
						infantry = { x = 1 y = 1 }
					}
				}
			}
			random_controlled_state = {
				limit = { is_in_home_area = yes }
				create_unit = {
					division = "name = \"Turkish Militia\" division_template = \"Turkish Militia\" start_experience_factor = 0.1"
					owner = PREV
					count = 5
					allow_spawning_on_enemy_provs = yes
				}
			}
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_in_faction = yes
					is_faction_leader = no
				}
				leave_faction = yes
			}
			if = {

				dismantle_faction = yes
			}
		}
